FNV VOLUMETRIC LOCAL-LIGHT MANAGER EPOCH CONTRACT FOLLOWUP

Required architecture:
1. OMV local-light values must remain available when bDrawShadows=0 and native shadow counts are zero.
2. Native shadow textures are optional per-light enrichment, never the local-light enumeration owner.
3. The render hook copies bounded scalar values only; it never retains a manager list node or native light pointer.

Closure questions:
1. Is manager +0xB4 a conventional node chain with next at +0 and ShadowSceneLight payload at +8?
2. Which functions insert, unlink, clear, destroy, or reassociate +0xB4 entries?
3. Can any mutation run concurrently with the world-frame call to 0x00B5B880?
4. Is 0x00B5B880 called even when native shadow drawing and both shadow counts are disabled?
5. At entry or return from 0x00B5B880, are +0xF8 native light, +0xF4 positional flag, +0xD0 multiplier, and native position/color/radius complete for the current world frame?
6. Which stable copied identity joins a scene-wide value record to an optional completed shadow record?
7. What bounded deterministic ordering matches the engine contribution score without retaining engine pointers?
8. Which loading, reset, camera, or scene transitions require publishing an explicit empty epoch?

Required result:
A proven zero-native-shadow snapshot boundary and copied-value ABI suitable for an always-available bounded OMV local-light path.
